Woman","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/DSC_2156.jpg?resize=780%2C520":null,"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/DSC_2226.jpg?resize=780%2C520":null,"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/DSC_2327.jpg?resize=780%2C520":null,"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/DSC_2414.jpg?resize=780%2C520":null,"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/pwcooks/~4/HgPUsiJ41TM":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn64@2020_6/2020/08/24/21-21-54-806_215e064174a3d805.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598304110519},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 05:21:50","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 05:21:50","title":"Tomato Soup 2.0 by The Pioneer Woman","link":"https://thepioneerwoman.com/?post_type=cooking&p=105228","description":"<p>As I have covered on <a href=\"http://thepioneerwoman.com/confessions\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" target=\"_blank\">Confessions</a>, the Drummond kids and I have been making the most of our time at home by filming episodes of my Food Network show in the Lodge kitchen. Episode 2 of this &#8220;Staying Home&#8221; series airs tomorrow morning (April 25) and I wanted to share one of the recipes from the show. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0302-1.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0302-1.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-105181\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0302-1.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=8256 8256w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0302-1.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0302-1.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0302-1.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0302-1.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0302-1.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0302-1.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0302-1.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0302-1.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>It&#8217;s called Tomato Soup 2.0 and basically takes generic condensed tomato soup and turns it into something you&#8217;d eat in Paris. And I&#8217;m not even sure if they have tomato soup in Paris, but if they do, they&#8217;re going to want to serve this recipe from now on!</p>\n<p>That made no sense.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0284.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0284.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-105179\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0284.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=8256 8256w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0284.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0284.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0284.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0284.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0284.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0284.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0284.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0284.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>You can see the step-by-step recipe on the show tomorrow, but here&#8217;s all you do:</p>\n<p>1. Heat a little olive oil in a saucepan over medium heat.<br />\n2. Add a couple of spoonfuls of jarred pesto. Stir it around and cook for a minute.<br />\n3. Add 2 large cans condensed tomato soup along with 2 cans of water.<br />\n4. Add a regular can of diced tomatoes with their juice. (I used tomatoes with oregano and garlic, but plain is fine.)<br />\n5. Stir and bring to a gentle simmer.<br />\n6. Add a generous splash of SHERRY! It is transformative. If you don&#8217;t have sherry, a little splash of white wine will do. (And I actually used cooking sherry, which is sold in supermarkets next to vinegar! Crazytown.) Stir and continue to heat the soup.<br />\n7. Add dried parsley, salt, and freshly ground black pepper. Stir.<br />\n8. Add grated parmesan and stir. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0303.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0303.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-105182\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0303.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=8256 8256w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0303.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0303.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0303.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0303.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0303.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0303.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0303.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/DSC_0303.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>9. Serve with garlic butter croutons and extra Parmesan on top. And guess what I used for the croutons? Frozen Garlic Texas Toast! I just cut the frozen pieces into cubes, sprinkled with grated Parmesan, and baked them according to the regular instructions on the package. They are amazing on the soup, and so crispy and delightful. </p>\n<p>My house is full of people, everyone wants to eat all the time, and I&#8217;m into easy food these days. Canned soup and frozen garlic bread for the win!</p>\n<p>&#8220;Staying Home: Episode 2&#8221; airs on Food Network this Saturday morning at 10am/9c&#8230;and I hope you enjoy the homemade feel of things. (I also hope you get a kick out of my accidentally setting a wooden spoon on fire&#8230;but you&#8217;ll have to tune in to see how that went. Ha.)</p>\n<p>And I hope you&#8217;re all doing okay. Sending lots and lots of love from the ranch.</p>\n<p>xoxo,<br />\nP-Dub</p>\n<img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/pwcooks/~4/NET7oNd1TOE\" height=\"1\" width=\"1\" Everything&#8212;from the seasoned roasted chicken to the tender autumnal veggies, to the luscious balsamic glaze to the crispy toast it&#8217;s served with&#8212;is just lovely. Winner, winner, chicken dinner and all that jazz. Here&#8217;s how to make it!</p>\n<p>Start by preheating the oven to 375. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2630.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2630.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103320\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2630.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=5568 5568w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2630.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2630.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2630.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2630.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2630.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2630.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2630.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, paprika, and chili powder in a small bowl&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2632.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2632.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103321\" 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2632.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2632.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2632.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2632.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2632.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2632.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2632.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Stir to mix it together. (You can have some fun with this spice mixture and spike it with whatever floats your boat. Curry powder, cayenne, the list goes on!)</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2633.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2633.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2633.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2633.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Lay out the chicken thighs on a plate or sheet pan&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2636.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2636.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2636.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, salt and pepper and rub the spice mixture all over it. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2639.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2639.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2639.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2639.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2639.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, squarsh (I love pronouncing it like that) into chunks (or you can buy it already cut up in some supermarkets!)&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2638.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2638.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Then cut a peeled red onion into chunks&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2642.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2642.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" I love them! Trim them and cut them in half. (And truth be told, I lop off the bottom and cut them in half first, which makes it easier to pull off the damaged outer leaves.) Or&#8230;yes. You can just buy them already trimmed and halved. What is the world coming to?</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2647.jpg?resize=780%2C1170\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2647.jpg?resize=780%2C1170\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"1170\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103328\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2647.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=3712 3712w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2647.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=200 200w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2647.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2647.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=683 683w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2647.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2647.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=1365 1365w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2647.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=1560 1560w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2647.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>For the herbiage (not to be confused with verbiage, which, unlike herbiage, is actually a word), grab some thyme, rosemary, and sage. Simon and Garfunkel would be 75% pleased with these choices! </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2648.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2648.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103329\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2648.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=5568 5568w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2648.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2648.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2648.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2648.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2648.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2648.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2648.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2648.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Pull the leaves off the thyme and rosemary, and stack it together with the sage leaves&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2649.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2649.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103330\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2649.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=5568 5568w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2649.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2649.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2649.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2649.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2649.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2649.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2649.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2649.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Then chop them pretty fine.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2650.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2650.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103331\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2650.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=5568 5568w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2650.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2650.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2650.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2650.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2650.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2650.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2650.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2650.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Time to start cookin&#8217;! Heat a large cast iron skillet over medium heat, then add a couple to three tablespoons olive oil. Grab the chicken with tongs&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2653.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2653.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103332\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2653.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=5568 5568w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2653.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2653.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2653.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2653.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2653.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2653.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2653.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2653.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>And place it skin side down in the skillet. Babysit the chicken to make sure the skin doesn&#8217;t stick to the skillet, and brown the first side for about 4 minutes.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2654.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2654.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103333\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2654.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=5568 5568w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2654.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2654.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2654.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2654.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2654.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2654.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2654.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2654.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Turn the chicken when the skin is nice and golden, then brown the second side for about 2 minutes. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2656.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2656.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103334\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2656.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=5568 5568w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2656.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2656.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2656.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2656.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2656.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2656.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2656.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2656.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Remove the chicken to a plate and set it aside&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2658.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2658.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103335\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2658.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=5568 5568w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2658.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2658.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2658.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2658.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2658.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2658.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2658.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2658.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>And pour off most of the excess grease. (You can always add some back in later if you miss it!)</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2659.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2659.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103336\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2659.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=5568 5568w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2659.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2659.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2659.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2659.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2659.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2659.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2659.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2659.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Throw a bunch of garlic cloves into the skillet (if the skillet seems too hot/smoky, you can reduce the heat to medium-low.) Stir them and cook them for a couple of minutes, making sure they don&#8217;t burn. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2660.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2660.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2660.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2660.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Add the onions and herbs&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2661.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2661.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2661.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2661.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>And stir them, cooking them for 2 to 3 minutes, being careful not to burn them.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2662.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2662.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2662.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2662.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Raise the heat to medium-high. Add the butternut squash, Brussels sprouts, and cauliflower (which I didn&#8217;t mention above, but here it is!) Sprinkle them with salt and pepper&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2663.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img about 3 minutes, allowing them to start to cook and get color around the edges.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2665.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2665.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Splash in some red wine (or, if you prefer, chicken broth)&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2667.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2667.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2667.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2667.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2667.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2667.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Then give the veggies one more stir.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2670.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2670.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103344\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2670.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=5568 5568w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2670.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2670.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2670.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2670.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2670.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2670.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2670.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2670.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Nestle the chicken into the veggies (use tongs to make room and move some of the veggies around as needed) and put the skillet into the oven for 25 minutes.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2673.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2673.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103345\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2673.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=5568 5568w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2673.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2673.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2673.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2673.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2673.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2673.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2673.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2673.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>While the chicken and veggies finish cooking in the oven, toast some good sliced bread in a skillet with lots of butter. Set them aside and tell your family it won&#8217;t be long, and that they can stop banking their forks and their heads on the dinner table. (Hypothetically speaking.)</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2675.jpg?resize=780%2C1170\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2675.jpg?resize=780%2C1170\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"1170\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103346\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2675.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=3712 3712w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2675.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=200 200w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2675.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2675.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=683 683w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2675.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2675.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=1365 1365w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2675.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=1560 1560w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2675.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Pull the skillet out of the oven&#8212;yum! I wrestled with whether to do 400 degrees or 375; I think at 400, the veggies might get a little more of that roasted color on the outside&#8230;but just follow your heart! Ha. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2676.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2676.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103347\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2676.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=5568 5568w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2676.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2676.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2676.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2676.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2676.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2676.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2676.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2676.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Serve up helpings of chicken, veggies, and toast (and a couple extra sage leaves)&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2681.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2681.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103348\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2681.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=5568 5568w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2681.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2681.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2681.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2681.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2681.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2681.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2681.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_2681.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Then drizzle on balsamic glaze (it&#8217;s sold in squeeze bottles in supermarkets now) and sprinkle with pomegranate seeds. The balsamic glaze adds a little sweetness and acidic bite, which really wakes everything up. Delicious! And you can have fun with this: Use sweet potatoes, turnips, and other root vegetables&#8230;or you can go rogue and add bell peppers, broccoli, mushrooms, whatever you like.</p>\n<p>Enjoy, 05:21:50","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 05:21:50","title":"Creamy Roasted Red Pepper Soup by The Pioneer Woman","link":"http://thepioneerwoman.com/?post_type=cooking&p=101129","description":"<p>Roasted red peppers are my favorite pantry item; well, they&#8217;re up there alongside jars of good marinara sauce. You can turn a jar or two of roasted red peppers into so many different recipes, from soups to sauces to panini to dips. The flavor is mild and slightly sweet, and I&#8217;m always amazed at how much I love them. This soup boasts two whole jars of the beauties, and it&#8217;s perfect for lunch or dinner. </p>\n<p>Plus, it&#8217;s purty. You&#8217;ll love it! </p>\n<p>(Side note: Hi, friends! *Waving*&#8230;)</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1608.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img oil and butter over medium heat.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1613.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img garlic&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1615.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img is optional; it helps with the texture, but you can leave it out if you&#8217;re wanting to cut carbs)&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a Flavah!</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1624.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img red bell peppers for about 3 more minutes.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1627.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img paste&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1630.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1630.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-101146\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1630.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1630.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1630.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1630.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1630.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>And stir to combine, letting it cook for a couple of minutes.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1632.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1632.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-101147\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1632.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1632.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1632.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1632.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1632.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Sprinkle in the salt and pepper and turn up the heat to medium-high.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1638.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1638.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-101148\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1638.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1638.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1638.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1638.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1638.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Pour in the white wine, then stir and let it start to cook.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1640.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1640.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-101149\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1640.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1640.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1640.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1640.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1640.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Then pour in some vegetable or chicken stock!</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1552.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1552.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-101130\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1552.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1552.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1552.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1552.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1552.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Bring the mixture to a gentle boil, then reduce the heat to medium-low and simmer until the potatoes are very tender, about 18-20 minutes.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1553.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1553.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-101131\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1553.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1553.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1553.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1553.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1553.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Now it&#8217;s time to puree the soup, which releases all the amazing flavor of the peppers and makes the potatoes just become a part of the mix.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1560.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1560.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-101132\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1560.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1560.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1560.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1560.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1560.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Keep going until it gets to the texture you like. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1562.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1562.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-101133\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1562.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1562.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1562.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1562.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1562.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>This is the texture I like!</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1566.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1566.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-101134\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1566.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1566.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1566.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1566.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1566.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Now it just needs cream. I add about a half a cup, or up to 5 gallons. Just kidding about the 5 gallon part, but my point is that if you wanna add more cream, you should live the life you were born to live and just add it.</p>\n<p>And truth be told, I probably added 3/4 cup of cream.</p>\n<p>Okay, a cup.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1569.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1569.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-101136\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1569.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1569.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1569.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1569.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1569.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Stir it to combine and let the cream warm up for a couple of minutes. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1571.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1571.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-101137\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1571.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1571.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1571.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1571.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1571.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Finally, add a little red wine vinegar and cook for another minutes. Done!</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1679.jpg?resize=780%2C1170\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1679.jpg?resize=780%2C1170\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"1170\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-101153\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1679.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1679.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=200 200w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1679.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1679.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=683 683w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Serve with a little grated Parmesan and some fresh oregano leaves. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1691.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1691.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-101156\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1691.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1691.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1691.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1691.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1691.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>A little grilled cheese rollup wouldn&#8217;t hurt either! (I&#8217;ll post these sometime soon.)</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1690.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1690.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-101155\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1690.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1690.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1690.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1690.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/dsc_1690.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Enjoy, friends! I&#8217;m sure Paige would agree with me if she would ever call me back. Ha. </p>\n<p>Happy Birthday, Paigie!!!</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n<strong>FOOD NETWORK UPDATE</strong></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/img_7865.jpg?resize=780%2C970\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/img_7865.jpg?resize=780%2C970\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"970\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-98947\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/img_7865.jpg?resize=780%2C970?w=1200 1200w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/img_7865.jpg?resize=780%2C970?w=241 241w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/img_7865.jpg?resize=780%2C970?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/img_7865.jpg?resize=780%2C970?w=824 824w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>There is a wacky rumor circulating around Facebook that I have decided to quit my Food Network show and devote my life to selling facial cream. The source of the rumor is an unscrupulous company trying to trick people into buying (you guessed it) facial cream. I have nothing to do with this facial cream (please don&#8217;t buy it!), and more importantly: I am not quitting my Food Network show! On the contrary: I&#8217;m just getting warmed up, man! The past seven years have just been one gigantic dress rehearsal! </p>\n<p>You want recipes, cookbooks, pretty plates, pans, and Basset Hound cookie jars? Head my way! </p>\n<p>You want facial cream? Head to Walmart, Ulta, Sephora, or a department store. Don&#8217;t head to Pioneer Woman. I get my facial cream at Walmart, Ulta, Sephora, and department stores! (Which is to say I rotate a lot. I think it&#8217;s healthier for the skin. Hey, maybe I should sell facial cream! Just kidding.)</p>\n<p>All this to say, it&#8217;s going to be a great fall on my Food Network show, which I ain&#8217;t even close to quittin&#8217;! From now until the end of the year, you&#8217;ll see a brand spanking new episode every Saturday morning at 10 am Eastern/9 am Central. (I think one exception to this is Thanksgiving weekend, but that&#8217;s the only break in new episodes.) I&#8217;m having so much fun with the new shows these days, and hope you&#8217;re loving the recipes! </p>\n<p>Recipe: <a href=\"https://www.foodnetwork.com/recipes/ree-drummond/ranch-pork-chop-sheet-pan-supper-5399499\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Ranch Pork Chop Sheet Pan Supper</a></p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/l3a2631.jpg?resize=780%2C1170\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/l3a2631.jpg?resize=780%2C1170\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"1170\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-98938\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/l3a2631.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=1200 1200w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/l3a2631.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=200 200w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/l3a2631.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/l3a2631.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=683 683w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/l3a2631.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=1024 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Between filming, planning my cookbook (more on this below!), the boys&#8217; football schedule, and a few other things I have going on this fall, that hasn&#8217;t left much time for me to post step-by-step recipes here on my blog. They&#8217;re a cooking appliance known as a &#8220;Multi Cooker&#8221; which means it has several different functions, its most notable (and useful, in my experience) being a pressure cooker. I have to say, I was a bit of a latecomer to the Instant Pot world. I am generally resistant to new electronic cooking appliances, because I&#8217;m old school and love a dutch oven and an iron skillet. But then my BFF Hyacinth, who is an Instant Pot evangelist, gave me one for my birthday last January. I&#8217;ve slowly but surely come to LOVE it, and noticed that I wasn&#8217;t ever putting it away in the pantry. />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1226.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1226.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99141\"
