240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1226.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>I want to sear the roast before I cook it, so I hit the &#8220;saute&#8221; button. This heats the bottom of the insert. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1227.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1227.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99142\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1227.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1227.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1227.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1227.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1227.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1227.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1227.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>While it heats up, season a chuck roast with nuttin&#8217; but salt and pepper.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1229.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1229.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99144\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1229.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1229.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1229.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1229.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1229.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1229.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1229.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>When the Instant Pot is ready to saute, it will say &#8220;Hot!&#8221;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1228.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1228.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99143\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1228.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1228.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1228.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1228.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1228.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1228.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1228.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>So pour in a little olive oil&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1234.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1234.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99145\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1234.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1234.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1234.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1234.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1234.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1234.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1234.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>And throw in the roast!</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1235.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1235.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99146\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1235.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1235.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1235.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1235.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1235.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1235.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1235.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>It&#8217;ll start to suh-MOKE and stu-EAM. It gets hot in there! Not quite as hot as a heated cast iron dutch oven&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1237.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1237.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99147\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1237.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1237.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1237.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1237.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1237.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1237.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1237.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>But definitely hot enough to brown the surface of the meat.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1238.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1238.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99148\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1238.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1238.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1238.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1238.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1238.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1238.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1238.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>When it&#8217;s browned on both sides, remove it to a plate. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1240.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1240.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99150\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1240.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1240.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1240.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1240.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1240.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1240.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1240.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Then throw some large chunks of onion right in. These are going to cook down to almost nothingness, so the bigger the pieces, the better.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1242.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1242.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99151\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1242.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1242.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1242.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1242.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1242.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1242.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1242.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Move the onions around for a couple of minutes and let them start to brown.</p>\n<p><em>Note: I would normally add carrots to my pot roast! But guess what? Some turkey in my house ate all my carrots. So imagine there are large carrot chunks in this beautiful Instant Pot, kay?</em></p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1245.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1245.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99152\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1245.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1245.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1245.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1245.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1245.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1245.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1245.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Now&#8217;s the time to add in some red wine. A little&#8230;or not a little. (Translation: About 1/2 cup.)</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1248.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1248.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99153\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1248.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1248.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1248.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1248.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1248.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1248.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1248.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Stir the onions, scraping up the bits from the bottom as much as you can. Let the wine cook for a minute or so&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1250.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1250.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99154\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1250.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1250.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1250.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1250.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1250.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1250.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1250.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Then pour in beef broth. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1251.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1251.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99155\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1251.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1251.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1251.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1251.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1251.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1251.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1251.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>I love rosemary and thyme in my pot roast!</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1252.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1252.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99156\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1252.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1252.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1252.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1252.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1252.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1252.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1252.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Chuck it right in, no need to chop.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1255.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1255.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99157\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1255.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1255.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1255.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1255.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1255.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1255.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1255.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Finally, the meat&#8212;as well as all the juices on the plate.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1256.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1256.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99158\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1256.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1256.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1256.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1256.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1256.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1256.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1256.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Now it&#8217;s time to pressure cook! Put the lid on. It locks closed, and you&#8217;ll know it&#8217;s locked when it emits a lovely little chime.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1258.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1258.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99159\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1258.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1258.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1258.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1258.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1258.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1258.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1258.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>This is the pressure valve. You want to make sure it&#8217;s in the &#8220;Sealing&#8221; position.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1260.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1260.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99160\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1260.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1260.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1260.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1260.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1260.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1260.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1260.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Push the &#8220;Manual&#8221; button.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1261.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1261.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99161\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1261.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1261.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1261.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1261.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1261.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1261.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1261.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Hit the plus sign until it gets to 60 minutes (hard to read in this photo, but it says &#8220;60&#8221;), then give it a few seconds&#8230;and it will start the pressure cooking process! And here&#8217;s what happens: After a little time, you will see some steam releasing from the valve in a steady stream. This is normal! The Instant Pot is releasing excess steam as it comes up to temperature. This can take several minutes.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1301.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1301.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99166\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1301.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1301.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1301.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1301.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1301.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1301.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1301.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>When this little button pops up, as pictured here, that means the unit is sealed and the pressure cooking has begun. From there, it will cook for 60 minutes. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1263.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1263.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99162\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1263.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1263.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1263.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1263.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1263.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1263.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1263.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Once the 60 minutes is done, the unit will automatically change to &#8220;Keep Warm.&#8221; During this time, the Instant Pot will remain locked and will begin naturally releasing pressure on its own. It is best not to disturb the process during this time.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1266.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1266.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99164\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1266.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1266.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1266.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1266.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1266.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1266.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1266.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Rather than counting down from 60 as it did when it was pressure cooking, the Instant Pot will now count up the minutes it is taking to release the pressure naturally. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1264.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1264.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99163\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1264.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1264.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1264.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1264.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1264.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1264.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1264.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>You have the option to use a spoon handle to manually push the valve to &#8220;Venting&#8221; to manually release the pressure. However, when I have the time, I try to let the Instant Pot release as much pressure naturally as possible before I release the rest of the pressure manually. I think the food is the better for it. </p>\n<p>After about 15 minutes of natural release, I&#8217;ll often go ahead and release the rest manually so I can get this show on the road!</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1300.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1300.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99165\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1300.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1300.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1300.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1300.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1300.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1300.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1300.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>When the steam is no longer coming out&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1302.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1302.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99167\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1302.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1302.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1302.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1302.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1302.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1302.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1302.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>The button will pop down, indicating the pressure has been released and it&#8217;s safe to open the lid.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1307.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1307.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1307.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1307.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1307.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1307.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>And look at that! It looks like a roast that&#8217;s been simmering away for 3-4 hours. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1311.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1311.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1311.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1311.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1311.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1311.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>The first thing I do is skim off as much fat as I can from the top before disturbing everything and mixing the fat in.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1314.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1314.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99170\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1314.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1314.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1314.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1314.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1314.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1314.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1314.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Um&#8230;look at this meat! It is absolutely falling apart. It&#8217;s a miracle.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1337.jpg?resize=780%2C1170\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1337.jpg?resize=780%2C1170\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"1170\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99174\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1337.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1337.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=200 200w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1337.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1337.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=683 683w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1337.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1337.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=1365 1365w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1337.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=1560 1560w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Serve big shreds of the pot roast with a side of mashed potatoes and the cooking liquid spooned over the roast. (Imagine this with big chunks of carrots!)</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1340.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1340.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-99176\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1340.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2000 2000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1340.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1340.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1340.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1340.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1340.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1340.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>I love my dutch oven. But I&#8217;m really loving my Instant Pot, too. It&#8217;s been fun to dive in and experiment. .com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1258.jpg?resize=780%2C520":null,"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1260.jpg?resize=780%2C520":null,"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1261.jpg?resize=780%2C520":null,"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1301.jpg?resize=780%2C520":null,"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1263.jpg?resize=780%2C520":null,"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1266.jpg?resize=780%2C520":null,"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1264.jpg?resize=780%2C520":null,"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1300.jpg?resize=780%2C520":null,"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1302.jpg?resize=780%2C520":null,"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1307.jpg?resize=780%2C520":null,"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1311.jpg?resize=780%2C520":null,"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1314.jpg?resize=780%2C520":null,"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/09/dsc_1337.jpg?resize=780%2C1170":null,"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/pwcooks/~4/aNzFXg92kJI":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn80@2020_2/2020/08/24/21-21-52-935_2e8b965234be9b1d.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598304110524},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 05:21:50","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 05:21:50","title":"Pork Rind Chicken Strips! by The Pioneer Woman","link":"https://thepioneerwoman.com/?post_type=cooking&p=103242","description":"<p>I&#8217;ve been excited to share these delightful chicken strips on my blog ever since I first made them earlier this year. They&#8217;re in my <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Pioneer-Woman-Cooks-Fantastic-Favorites/dp/0062561375/ref=pd_sbs_14_5/139-5517632-4480509?_encoding=UTF8&#038;pd_rd_i=0062561375&#038;pd_rd_r=8d65c5af-a23e-11e9-8d7b-65f6631cf204&#038;pd_rd_w=ZTjfb&#038;pd_rd_wg=7iO5s&#038;pf_rd_p=588939de-d3f8-42f1-a3d8-d556eae5797d&#038;pf_rd_r=T8P0MQQ8683CGZ0RJ2N7&#038;psc=1&#038;refRID=T8P0MQQ8683CGZ0RJ2N7\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" target=\"_blank\">new cookbook</a>, and if you can get past the initial weirdness of the recipe title, you will become absolutely smitten with how tasty they are. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/rinds.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/rinds.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103273\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/rinds.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=5568 5568w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/rinds.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/rinds.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/rinds.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/rinds.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/rinds.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/rinds.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/rinds.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/rinds.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>First: About pork rinds! As I write in my cookbook, they have long been relegated to the snack/chip aisle in the grocery store, but when the low carb/Keto revolution happened, people discovered that, when ground up, they make the most magical stand-in for breadcrumbs. (It gets even more fun when you consider that pork rinds now come in lots of different flavors, like regular chips.) Pork rinds as chicken strip breading is definitely one of those &#8220;who thinks these things up?!?&#8221; scenarios&#8212;kind of like the person who decided to try putting Preparation H. under their eyes to reduce swelling. Note that I did not write that comment about Preparation H. in my cookbook. It&#8217;s a good thing I still have my wits about me in some areas!</p>\n<p>Anyway, I encourage you to give these a try! This pork rind breading can be used to bread pretty much anything you&#8217;d normally coat in breadcrumbs: fish sticks, fried mozzarella, the list goes on. Also, it&#8217;s just really fun to say &#8220;I made pork rind chicken strips&#8221; and watch the confused fascination that appears on the listener&#8217;s face. </p>\n<p>Here&#8217;s how to make them!</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4842.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4842.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103243\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4842.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2500 2500w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4842.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4842.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4842.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4842.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4842.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4842.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4842.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4842.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Cut 2 boneless, skinless chicken breasts into thin strips. You can also buy a package of chicken tenders if you prefer!</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4845.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4845.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103245\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4845.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2500 2500w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4845.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4845.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4845.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4845.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4845.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4845.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4845.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4845.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Place them into a bag or bowl and pour in buttermilk&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4847.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4847.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103246\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4847.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2500 2500w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4847.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4847.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4847.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4847.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4847.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4847.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4847.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4847.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Along with some hot sauce, salt and pepper. Easy!</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4849.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4849.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103247\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4849.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2500 2500w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4849.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4849.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4849.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4849.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4849.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4849.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4849.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4849.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Seal the bag and just smush (or stir, if it&#8217;s in a bowl) it around until the chicken is all coated. Set it aside.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4850.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4850.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103248\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4850.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2500 2500w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4850.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4850.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4850.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4850.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4850.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4850.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4850.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4850.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Now comes the fun, pork rindy part! In a separate bag or bowl, add some pork rinds&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4853.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4853.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103250\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4853.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2500 2500w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4853.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4853.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4853.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4853.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4853.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4853.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4853.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4853.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Then crunch/crush them until they become little crumbs! Some bigger chunks are fine. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4854.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4854.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103251\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4854.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2500 2500w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4854.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4854.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4854.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4854.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4854.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4854.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4854.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4854.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Pour them into a bowl&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4857.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4857.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103253\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4857.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2500 2500w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4857.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4857.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4857.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4857.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4857.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4857.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4857.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, a couple of beaten eggs. That&#8217;s the breading assembly line! (So easy, isn&#8217;t it?)</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4858.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4858.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2500 2500w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4858.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 chicken, lay one of the strips in the pork rinds&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4860.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img coat&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4862.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4862.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103257\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4862.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2500 2500w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4862.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4862.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4862.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4862.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4862.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4862.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4862.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4862.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Quickly dunk it in the egg&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4863.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4863.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103258\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4863.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2500 2500w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4863.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4863.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4863.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4863.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4863.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4863.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4863.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4863.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>And put it back in the crumbs to coat, pressing to make as many crumbs stick as possible. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4865.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4865.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103259\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4865.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2500 2500w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4865.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4865.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4865.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4865.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4865.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4865.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4865.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4865.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Lay them on a sheet pan as you go. Look at how crispy and fun!</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4878.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4878.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103263\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4878.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2500 2500w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4878.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4878.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4878.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4878.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4878.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4878.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4878.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4878.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>When they&#8217;re all coated, heat 1 inch of vegetable oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4880.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4880.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103264\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4880.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2500 2500w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4880.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4880.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4880.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4880.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4880.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4880.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4880.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4880.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Working in batches of 2 or 3, lay the strips in the oil and fry for about 2 to 2 1/2 minutes on the first side&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4882.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4882.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103265\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4882.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2500 2500w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4882.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4882.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4882.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4882.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4882.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4882.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4882.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4882.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Then flip them over and fry them for a couple of minutes on the second side, until golden and crisp. You&#8217;ll want to babysit these, moving them around with tongs to make sure they don&#8217;t burn. You can lower the heat to medium if it looks like the pork rinds are getting too brown! </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4885.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4885.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103266\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4885.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2500 2500w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4885.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4885.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4885.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4885.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4885.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4885.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4885.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4885.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Remove to a rack while you fry the rest.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4874.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4874.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103262\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4874.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2500 2500w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4874.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1024 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4874.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4874.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 2048w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4874.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4874.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_4874.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2340 2340w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Now, if you&#8217;re a normal consumer of chicken strips, you can serve them right away with ketchup and/or ranch. But I make a really nice creamy avocado sauce that kinda rocked my world: In a food processor, add avocado, mayonnaise, fresh dill, garlic, lime juice, salt, and pepper. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_9389.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_9389.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-103269\" 1024w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_9389.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1536 1536w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/DSC_9389.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=2048 it&#8217;s a light green masterpiece!</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/PorkRindChickenStrips1.jpg?resize=780%2C1170\"><img go, my friends. Chicken strips coated in pork rinds, what is this world coming to?</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a 05:21:50","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 05:21:50","title":"Mini Turtle Cheesecakes by The Pioneer Woman","link":"http://thepioneerwoman.com/?post_type=cooking&p=100270","description":"<p>I love cheesecake, but sometimes I can&#8217;t be bothered to make a big, honking full-sized one. I don&#8217;t know what the mental block is, but if I have the idea &#8220;Hey! I think I&#8217;ll make a cheesecake!&#8221; I immediately get really tired and want to get back in bed. I think it&#8217;s partly to do with the fact that a full-sized cheesecake is a living, breathing thing, and while I can usually avoid winding up with a big crack down the middle, sometimes a cheesecake does what it wants to do. In addition, a full-sized cheesecake takes so long to chill properly, and by the time you can actually cut a slice and enjoy it, you have now aged 27 years. </p>\n<p>As I said, I just want to get back in bed.</p>\n<p>So mini cheesecakes are where I live! They&#8217;re simpler, provide more immediate gratification (relatively speaking) and you can freeze them and just pull out what you need when you need it. </p>\n<p>And they don&#8217;t make me tired. Sold! </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2597.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2597.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100234\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2597.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2597.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2597.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2597.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2597.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>First, make the chocolate cookie crust. Add chocolate graham crackers to a food processor. (Or you can use Oreos!)</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2599.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2599.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100235\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2599.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2599.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2599.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2599.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2599.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Add a little sugar&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2601.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2601.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100236\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2601.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2601.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2601.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2601.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2601.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Then pulse the crumbs&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2603.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2603.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100269\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2603.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2603.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2603.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2603.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2603.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Until they&#8217;re really fine. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2605.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2605.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100268\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2605.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2605.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2605.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2605.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2605.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Keep pulsing while you drizzle in melted butter. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2606.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2606.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100237\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2606.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2606.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2606.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2606.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2606.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>This makes the crumbs nice and moist.</p>\n<p>Oh, and buttery!</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2608.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2608.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100238\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2608.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2608.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2608.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2608.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2608.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Line a couple of muffin pans with paper cups, then add crumbs to each one. You need about 2 tablespoons of crumbs in each cup.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2610.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2610.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100239\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2610.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2610.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2610.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2610.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2610.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Use your fangers or the bottom of a 1/4 cup measure to pack them tightly in the cups.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2614.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2614.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100240\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2614.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2614.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2614.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2614.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2614.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Now just set these aside; no need to bake &#8217;em!</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2616.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2616.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100241\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2616.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2616.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2616.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2616.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2616.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Next up: Make the cream cheese filling! That&#8217;s softened cream cheese&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2619.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2619.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100266\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2619.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2619.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2619.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2619.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2619.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Sugar&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2620.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2620.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100267\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2620.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2620.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2620.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2620.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2620.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>And eggs. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2624.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2624.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100243\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2624.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2624.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300
