https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2624.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Oh! And vanilla!</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2622.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2622.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100242\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2622.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2622.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2622.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2622.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2622.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Beat this until it&#8217;s totally smooth&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2627.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2627.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100244\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2627.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2627.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2627.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2627.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2627.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Then (this is where things really go off the rails) drizzle in some jarred salted caramel. (If you can&#8217;t find salted caramel sauce, you can just use regular caramel sauce with a little salt added.)</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2631.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2631.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100245\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2631.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2631.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2631.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2631.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2631.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Mix this in, scraping the sides of the bowl and trying really hard not to dive in and eat this with a spoon. Just remember everything your mama taught you about patience being a virtue! </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2635.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2635.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100246\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2635.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2635.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2635.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2635.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2635.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Divide the batter equally among the muffin cups.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2639.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2639.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100264\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2639.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2639.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2639.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2639.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2639.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>It should work out to be roughtly 3 tablespoons of batter per cup. Give or take a gallon.</p>\n<p>Now put these into a preheated 350 degree oven and bake them for about 15 to 17 minutes, until they&#8217;re set.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2594.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2594.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100233\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2594.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2594.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2594.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2594.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2594.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Let them cool for a bit, then pop the pans into the fridge to chill completely, about 2 hours or so. (Or you can make these and keep them in the fridge overnight if you have a life to go live!)</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2642.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2642.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100247\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2642.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2642.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2642.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2642.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2642.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>When the cheesecakes are chilled and you&#8217;re ready to finish them, make a luscious and easy ganache: Add chopped semisweet chocolate to a bowl&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2645.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2645.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100248\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2645.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2645.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2645.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2645.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2645.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Then pour over hot heavy cream&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2646.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2646.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100249\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2646.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2646.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2646.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2646.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2646.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>And let it sit for a couple of minutes.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2649.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2649.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100250\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2649.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2649.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2649.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2649.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2649.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Once the chocolate has started to soften, start whisking it slowly&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2651.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2651.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100251\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2651.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2651.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2651.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2651.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2651.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>And keep going until the mixture is smooth and perfect. This is a slightly thick ganache; you can add a little more cream if you want it to be a little thinner.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2660.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2660.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100252\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2660.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2660.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2660.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2660.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2660.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Add a little ganache to the tops of the chilled cheesecakes and spread it to even it out.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2662.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2662.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100253\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2662.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2662.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2662.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2662.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2662.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Lightly press a pecan half in the center&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2663.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2663.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100254\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2663.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2663.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2663.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2663.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2663.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Then sprinkle mini chocolate chips all over. </p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2665.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2665.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100255\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2665.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2665.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2665.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2665.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2665.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>The straw that broke the camel&#8217;s back is a little more salted caramel sauce on top! Don&#8217;t try to be neat about it; if it gets on the paper cup, great. Life is beautifully messy.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2673.jpg?resize=780%2C1170\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2673.jpg?resize=780%2C1170\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"1170\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100256\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2673.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2673.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=200 200w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2673.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2673.jpg?resize=780%2C1170?w=683 683w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>You can freeze these in the finished form, then just pull them out and let them thaw. Or you can chill them in the fridge and serve them later in the day.</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2753.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2753.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100258\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2753.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2753.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2753.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2753.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2753.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>Or&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#160;<br />\n&#160;<br />\n<a href=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2755.jpg?resize=780%2C520\"><img src=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2755.jpg?resize=780%2C520\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"520\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-100259\" srcset=\"https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2755.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=1000 1000w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2755.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=300 300w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2755.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=768 768w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2755.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=240 240w, https://thepioneerwoman.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/dsc_2755.jpg?resize=780%2C520?w=480 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a>You can just dive in right now. </p>\n<p>As you can see, that&#8217;s exactly what I did. </p>\n<p>Enjoy these, friends!
